## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Streams DSL to Processor API Migration

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the Kafka Streams DSL (map, filter, groupBy) and their corresponding Processor API equivalents, to support a team migrating from DSL to lower-level Processor API for custom state store management.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

I am thinking...: Let me now compile the comprehensive list of files I've found. The task is to find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the Kafka Streams DSL (map, filter, groupBy) and their corresponding Processor API equivalents.

The key files I've found are:

**DSL Interface files (public API):**
1. `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/KStream.java` - DSL interface with filter, map, groupBy, etc.
2. `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/KTable.java` - DSL interface with filter, mapValues, groupBy
3. `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/KGroupedStream.java` - DSL interface for grouped stream operations

582026-03-08T21:17:45.065749agentmessage-
`/workspace/answer.json` is written and valid. Here is a full narrative of every finding, organized for your migration team:

---

## Complete DSL → Processor API File Map for Apache Kafka Streams

All paths are relative to `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/`.

---

### 1. Processor API Core Interfaces (`processor/api/`)

These are the contracts your custom processors must implement:

| File | Role |
|---|---|
| `Processor.java` | Core interface for key-changing processors. Implement `process(Record<KIn,VIn>)`. |
| `ProcessorSupplier.java` | Factory for `Processor`. Override `stores()` to declare state store dependencies. Register with `Topology.addProcessor()`. |
| `FixedKeyProcessor.java` | Variant of `Processor` for operations that **never change the key** (filter, mapValues, peek). |
| `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java` | Factory for `FixedKeyProcessor`. |
| `ContextualProcessor.java` | Abstract base class implementing `Processor` — stores `ProcessorContext` for you. **Extend this** instead of implementing `Processor` directly. |
| `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java` | Same as above for `FixedKeyProcessor`. |
| `ProcessorContext.java` | Available in `init()`. Provides `getStateStore()`, `forward()`, `schedule()`, record metadata. |
| `FixedKeyProcessorContext.java` | Same as `ProcessorContext` but typed for fixed-key processors. |
| `Record.java` / `FixedKeyRecord.java` | Immutable record passed to `process()`. Use `withKey()`/`withValue()` to create modified copies for forwarding. |

---

### 2. DSL Interfaces (`kstream/`)

| File | DSL Operations Defined |
|---|---|
| `KStream.java` | `filter`, `map`, `mapValues`, `flatMap`, `flatMapValues`, `groupBy`, `groupByKey`, `join`, `leftJoin`, `outerJoin`, `peek`, `foreach`, `split`, `process`, `processValues` 
... (truncated)
